name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe Garden View Room Twin Bed
info:Stayed in September 2022
info:Family
info:1 Review
rating:1.7
posted:Posted September 14, 2022
msg:I saw this hotel in **. Since I often book rooms on Ctrip, I came here to place an order and earn some points! I ordered the Mid-Autumn Festival package (as shown in the picture below). I saw that the recommended programs were quite rich, and it was not easy to go out due to the epidemic, so I brought two families and children to experience it.

When I just checked into the hotel, I felt it was pretty good. The room was clean, the sheets were changed, and the front desk reception was also very enthusiastic. They gave us moon cakes and lion key chains, and told us that the hotel has a swimming pool on the seventh floor where we can take our children to play, and there will be VR game experience from 4 to 5 pm. As a result, when we came to the swimming pool, we found that this swimming pool was very small and there were super many people. You can imagine the scene of people next to each other. So we didn't swim, and went shopping at Guangbai downstairs.

At four o'clock, I brought three children to the entrance of the buffet restaurant on the sixth floor to play VR. There was only one machine here, and each person had a five-minute experience. We lined up until four-fifty-five, and the machine suddenly broke down. The waiter said that there was no electricity... We couldn't play... At this time, there was still half an hour before the buffet time, and we were too lazy to go up and down, so we sat on the stool at the entrance of the buffet restaurant and chatted. (During this period, I walked around the hotel. It was very small and there was no place to walk. The so-called cinema was just a few rows of chairs in the conference room. It was not very comfortable. It seemed that there would be a cartoon in the evening.) At about five-twenty, the restaurant staff came to tell us that the buffet was about to start and asked us to go out and wait. I said that we had already booked a buffet seat when we just checked in, and we also paid the difference for an adult (usually 168/person, Mid-Autumn Festival 198/person). Can we go in and sit first? Anyway, there are only ten minutes left. He said no, we must go out and wait. So we also cooperated and waited outside.

As it was almost time for dinner, more and more guests came to eat, and the seats at the entrance were almost full... We were at the back at this time, and I don't know how to describe it. In short, the scene was very chaotic... To be honest, I took my children to several hotel buffets during the holidays. The customer service can look up my comments on other hotels. The "entry method" of this hotel's buffet really needs to be improved...

After finally getting in, we found that the seat we originally reserved... was taken by someone else... This, this, this... If you can sit anywhere, what's the point of booking... After some communication, we sat down and started to eat. Maybe it was because of the holiday, there were so many people dining, and there was a queue for salmon, barbecue, steak, and ice cream... Because we had children, we symbolically queued once at the ice cream stall and didn't go, so we only ate things that didn't require queuing. After about seven o'clock, I saw that there was no one at the fish stall, so I went there, but there was no salmon... Later, I looked and saw that they didn't even have drinking cups, and used paper cups instead. The food supply started to be insufficient after seven o'clock, and the barbecue stall was also closed at about the same time.

Because the buffet experience the night before was not good, I didn't go to have breakfast the next day. Other family members went and came back saying that there was no milk... Alas! To sum up, the hotel is small, the restaurant is small, and we didn't seem to have tried the things that can be experienced in the set meal. In short, it's hard to say! The only thing I can comfort myself is that this price is indeed very attractive nowadays. As for the rest, well... you get what you pay for!
